<div id="review_1496363029" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1496363029" />
    <a title="Helen 2.0" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39575951-helen-2-0"><img alt="Helen 2.0" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460553725p2/39575951.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1496363029?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Helen 2.0" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Helen 2.0" href="/user/show/39575951-helen-2-0">Helen 2.0</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=brs-done">brs-done</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=retelling">retelling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=read-16">read-16</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1496363029" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11318121196146485444">Wonderland and madness and creepy crawling creatures is what I'm reading this series for. Unfortunately, there was less Wonderland and madness in Unhinged than in Splintered, but it did involve an animated clown doll that made me want to burn every toy I've ever owned out of sheer terror. Yes, that's what really makes me want to keep reading - sheer terror.<br/><br/>Morpheus remains the most interesting character in the series. As Alyssa herself points out, Morpheus always gets screwed when he does the ri</span>
  <span id="freeText11318121196146485444" style="display:none">Wonderland and madness and creepy crawling creatures is what I'm reading this series for. Unfortunately, there was less Wonderland and madness in Unhinged than in Splintered, but it did involve an animated clown doll that made me want to burn every toy I've ever owned out of sheer terror. Yes, that's what really makes me want to keep reading - sheer terror.<br /><br />Morpheus remains the most interesting character in the series. As Alyssa herself points out, Morpheus always gets screwed when he does the right thing, so he's learned to act selfishly and be manipulative to get what he wants. Even that isn't true - poor Morpheus suffers not so much from doing the right thing but from being misunderstood and second-guessed at every turn by the people he values (really just Alyssa). His motives aren't questionable but still end up being questioned.<br /><br />Alyssa sunk pretty low in Unhinged. Her narration wasn't frustrating, but her actions were. She spends the whole book trying to keep both Jeb and Morpheus on her hook while not truly committing to either. At one point, she promises her human life to Jeb, then <i>in the same chapter</i> she tells Morpheus to wait for her, because she plans to share forever with him. It was hard to root for a main character that treats the people she cares for so badly. Alyssa also mistreats her father, who worries himself sick over Aly; she doesn't seem to understand how horrible her father must feel, watching his daughter slowly spiral down into insanity just as he watched his wife years ago. Poor guy.<br /><br />All in all, not life-changing but pretty much as good as Splintered. I'm thinking I'll finish the series for closure and to hear more from Morpheus and the evil clown doll.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11318121196146485444" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_780593882" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/780593882" />
    <a title="C.G. Drews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews"><img alt="C.G. Drews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521552918p2/11375137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/780593882?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=best-of-2014">best-of-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=magical-fantasy">magical-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2014">read-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=retelling">retelling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer780593882" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12017087907240271233"><b> My mind = blown. </b> I'm just...gah, I have such a book hangover right now. I just want to fangirl and cry and stroke the book (preciousssss) and get on my hands and knees (not a normal position for me) and beg for the next book. Time, please go faster.<br/><br/><b> I mostly have the same loves and hates for Unhinged as I did with Splintered. </b> While I adored the creepiness of Wonderland (scootch over Tim Burton), I really didn't like how it was continually said "but Lewis Carroll got it wrong and instead it's </span>
  <span id="freeText12017087907240271233" style="display:none"><b> My mind = blown. </b> I'm just...gah, I have such a book hangover right now. I just want to fangirl and cry and stroke the book (preciousssss) and get on my hands and knees (not a normal position for me) and beg for the next book. Time, please go faster.<br><br><b> I mostly have the same loves and hates for Unhinged as I did with Splintered. </b> While I adored the creepiness of Wonderland (scootch over Tim Burton), I really didn't like how it was continually said "but Lewis Carroll got it wrong and instead it's like this...etc." No. Imagine my grumpy face (it's quite scary, actually) because Alice in Wonderland is my favourite classic of ever (besides Peter Pan) and while I love the continuation of the Splintered series, I don't like the dismissal of Lewis Carroll getting it "wrong"<br><br>That saying, the author does dedicate the book to Lewis Carroll in the acknowledgements.<br><br>Okay, picky stuff out the way, now let's get to the characters. <b> Oh my delicious characters. </b> (That sounded creepy, but Wonderland is all about the creepy.) While most of Splintered happened in Wonderland, most of Unhinged happens in our world. Bummer. I like Wonderland better. But did it lessen the awesome? Heck, no. There is CREEPINESS. There is mind-blowing IMAGINATION. There is MAGIC. Magic everywhere! <br><br>I'll say it again: <b> the author has the wickedest most fabulous imagination ever.</b> I'm in awe. I love the Wonderland she's created and how she adds layers and more layers and the amazingness just increases.<br><br>Of course then she used her imagination to hurt my babies. Happiness gone. DON'T HURT THEM.<br><br>Shall we talk characters now? Okay, good. I hoped you'd scream yes like that.<br><br><b> Alyssa </b><br>To be perfectly blunt (as I am sometimes), Al isn't my favourite narrator of ever. I like her! Don't get me wrong! But...she made a lot of stupid mistakes (a.k.a not dropping everything in Splintered and running to Morpheus's creepy arms). And she tended to see what she wanted to see. For a girl with the power of Wonderland at her fingertips she spent a lot of time ignoring it. Silly girl. <br><br>Also I was sad how she fought with her mother. You just got her back! But THAT, dear blogglings, made sense towards the end. <br><br><b> Jeb </b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378557ra/734234.gif" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Why...um, just why is he here? Life would be a whole lot simpler if Jeb just dropped off the face of the book. (Yeah, books aren't fun when they're simple, blah, blah.) Jeb spends a lot of time a) in the way, b) being his normal controlling self, and c) needing to be rescued. <br><br><b> Morpheus </b><br>Oh. Morpheus. But I won't blather unnecessarily about him, I promise. (You all know my feelings on this triangle.) My mind has exploded with Morpheus' plot twists. I spent the whole book saying, "Aw, Morpheus" and "AW MORPHEUS", which is the same phrase but the inflections are completely different. Sassy wit = vulnerable. Oh, and Morpheus got a car. <br><br>Morpheus and his car, basically:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395305126ra/8976763.gif" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I like that. I like that a lot.<br><br><b> The description was as awesome as always. </b> Seriously, I taste, see, smell, and feel so much. It's incredible. There are only a few books that I get so absorbed in while reading. This series is top of the list.<br><br><b> But talk about the cliffhanger ending. </b> HEY. Not. Fair. How...how can it end like that? It's so wrong...and completely right. And I will literally hyperventilate until 2015. You see if I don't.<br><br><b> I loved Unhinged. I just...I'm absolutely obsessed with this series, okay? </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395305126ra/8976764.gif" width="300" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="12017087907240271233" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/548048995?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/3659131-michelle">Michelle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548048995" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6777942429252146253">This is how I feel about this book<br/><br/><a href='http://s560.beta.photobucket.com/user/xxselxyxx/media/animated/HappyDance.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/340379.gif' alt=' photo HappyDance.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>****Update 9th Jan 2014****<br/><br/>While I have been anticipating <b>Unhinged</b> and getting to read it, part of me was worried it wouldn't live up the hype and reach my expectations. I fell in love with Splintered, the world and the characters, and each time I fall head over heels in love with a book I always worry that the second one won't meet its predecessor's standards. I really did not think I would love <b>Unhinged</b> as much as I did, or even love it more than Splintere</span>
  <span id="freeText6777942429252146253" style="display:none">This is how I feel about this book<br><br><a href="http://s560.beta.photobucket.com/user/xxselxyxx/media/animated/HappyDance.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/340379.gif" alt=" photo HappyDance.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>****Update 9th Jan 2014****<br><br>While I have been anticipating <b>Unhinged</b> and getting to read it, part of me was worried it wouldn't live up the hype and reach my expectations. I fell in love with Splintered, the world and the characters, and each time I fall head over heels in love with a book I always worry that the second one won't meet its predecessor's standards. I really did not think I would love <b>Unhinged</b> as much as I did, or even love it more than Splintered, but I was completely and utterly blown away by <b>Unhinged</b>.<br><br><b>Unhinged</b> hooked me from the minute I had the book in my hands and saw how amazingly gorgeous the cover is...go on, take another look........see what I mean ;). By the time I had reached the half way point in <b>Unhinged</b> I had so many emotions swirling around. I hated Morpheus for doing what he does to Alyssa, but liked how he has her back and saves her. Jeb just needed a serious kick in the ass, he has a good thing with Alyssa and is thinking too much with his business brain and not his emotional brain, not thinking of what he does for work will affect their relationship. Let's not start on Alyssa and what she is doing with both of these boys, lying to 'protect' Jeb, but being 'more than friends' friendly with Morpheus. I mean seriously, this trio are beyond messed up, but mostly in a good way, and in a way that wants you to keep reading and get tangled up in this mess with them.<br><br>There were a lot of twists and shocks in <b>Unhinged</b> that I didn't expect, and some of Alyssa's family history is revealed and explains a lot of why Alyssa is who she is. When I began reading I hated Alyssa's Mum for hiding a lot of this information from Alyssa to protect her, but then just as we near the end of the book we are actually shown what happened and why Alyssa's Mum made these choices.<br><br>I loved not knowing what was going to happen throughout <b>Unhinged</b>. The unpredictability of what would happen between Morpheus/Alyssa/Jeb had me turning page after page to get even the smallest hint about what was coming up, looking for any minute detail that would aid me in making this discovery. A. G. Howard makes you believe on thing, then pulls the rabbit out of the hat and erases what you thought you knew and shows you a whole new event.<br><br>Everyone in <b>Unhinged</b> has to go through so much, and the journey isn't easy at all. I loved following Alyssa through the glass, and down the rabbit hole. Being with her along her journey of discovery, seeing all the good and bad parts to Wonderland, but also finding out more about how it works.<br>The whole idea of the train was fantastic, and I could possibly do with one of them myself, and although I had guessed who the person was I was still surprised when it was revealed, like gasp out loud surprised. The last few chapters of <b>Unhinged</b> had me on the edge of my seat, I loved seeing them work as a team, but also seeing how they could be affected by everything that Wonderland is doing. How can it end like that, and the wait is going to be torture, like a year long torture specially designed to keep us hanging.<br></span>

<div id="review_548096179" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/548096179" />
    <a title="Stephanie (Bookfever)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4939266-stephanie-bookfever"><img alt="Stephanie (Bookfever)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595589358p2/4939266.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/548096179?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stephanie (Bookfever)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stephanie (Bookfever)" href="/user/show/4939266-stephanie-bookfever">Stephanie (Bookfever)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781419710476" href="/book/show/19430954-unhinged">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4939266-stephanie-bookfever?shelf=2014-publication">2014-publication</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4939266-stephanie-bookfever?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4939266-stephanie-bookfever?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4939266-stephanie-bookfever?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4939266-stephanie-bookfever?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4939266-stephanie-bookfever?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4939266-stephanie-bookfever?shelf=owned-physical-books">owned-physical-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548096179" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10977013138421090762">Wow! Unhinged was so damn good! I'm really impressed by how much I ended up loving it. It's been so freaking long since I read Splintered. Almost one year and a half I think so it's been really nice to get back into this amazing world. I had to stop a few times, though, to read some books that were due for review but I finally finished it and let me just say that I can't wait until the third book is out. I need it now!<br/><br/>It's a little hard to form any coherent thoughts with the way Unhinged ended. </span>
  <span id="freeText10977013138421090762" style="display:none">Wow! Unhinged was so damn good! I'm really impressed by how much I ended up loving it. It's been so freaking long since I read Splintered. Almost one year and a half I think so it's been really nice to get back into this amazing world. I had to stop a few times, though, to read some books that were due for review but I finally finished it and let me just say that I can't wait until the third book is out. I need it now!<br /><br />It's a little hard to form any coherent thoughts with the way Unhinged ended. Really, just everything that happened in this book was non-stop action, mystery and of course a bit of romance. Speaking of the romance. I am not a fan of love triangles but I can truly see Alyssa's hesitation between Jeb and Morpheus. Which is really weird because I'm a huge Morpheus fangirl. Moths FTW! And may I just say that in this book he was especially amazing. I mean wow. I love him. And I really want him to end up with Alyssa someday. <br />But throughout this book I've been growing a bit fonder of Jeb too. Imagine that.<br /><br />Alyssa has definitely grown as a character in my eyes. At the start of the book she thought she was done with all things Wonderland and ready to move on with Jeb. But of course things didn't go as planned at all. And I'm glad that eventually Alyssa finally found out for herself who she is and really believed it. You go, girl!<br /><br />And the story... it was brilliant. A.G. Howard is a fantastic writer. I love her writing style so much. It's beautiful, poetic and yet dark and creepy. Oh this book was so creepy. I loved it! <br />I also really liked the little twists involving Alyssa's mom and dad. Their past together and how it wasn't all how it seemed. It was a pretty unexpected turn of events and I loved every bit of that!<br /><br />What else can I say than I loved this book? I can't wait for Ensared to come out and find out how the story will continue from here on because the ending? Oh my god! I can't believe all that happened and those are the best books out there, that leave you shocked and breathless and aching for the next book. <br /><br />So five stars definitely earned for Unhinged by A.G. Howard!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10977013138421090762" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review548096179">

<div id="review_1100478586" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1100478586" />
    <a title="Katerina  Kondrenko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36306002-katerina-kondrenko"><img alt="Katerina  Kondrenko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590049412p2/36306002.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1100478586?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina  Kondrenko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina  Kondrenko" href="/user/show/36306002-katerina-kondrenko">Katerina  Kondrenko</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1100478586" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14847730650171268357"><b>
  <blockquote>4 out of 10</blockquote>
</b><br/><b>Ревью в моем блоге/This review on my blog<br/><a href='http://living-a-thousand-lives.blogspot.ru/2015/11/unhinged-by-ag-howard.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Living A Thousand Lives</a></b> <i>(please use Chrome/Yandex browser or Android/IOS to see the page; otherwise, spoiler-tags I use to make my post compact may not work)</i><br/> <br/><b>Short-Soundtrack:</b><br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=AOP26WOOMbc' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Marshall Crutcher – Main Theme</a><br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fY-d951-jas' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Coil – Red Queen</a><br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wh7tSaPjxTg' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ruelle – Everything Is Lost</a><br/><br/><b>Genre</b>: retelling, YA<br/><b>Stuff</b>: real world mixed up with netherlings<br/><b>Fail</b>: humans, school, Jeb, Jeb...Jeb.<br/><b>WOW</b>: Morpheus, still and always<br/><b>POV</b>: 1st-person, female<br/><b>Love-Geometry</b>: medium going to hard<br/><br/><b>Quote-C</b></span>
  <span id="freeText14847730650171268357" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>4 out of 10</blockquote>
</b><br><b>Ревью в моем блоге/This review on my blog<br><a href="http://living-a-thousand-lives.blogspot.ru/2015/11/unhinged-by-ag-howard.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Living A Thousand Lives</a></b> <i>(please use Chrome/Yandex browser or Android/IOS to see the page; otherwise, spoiler-tags I use to make my post compact may not work)</i><br> <br><b>Short-Soundtrack:</b><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=AOP26WOOMbc" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Marshall Crutcher – Main Theme</a><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fY-d951-jas" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Coil – Red Queen</a><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wh7tSaPjxTg" rel="nofollow noopener">Ruelle – Everything Is Lost</a><br><br><b>Genre</b>: retelling, YA<br><b>Stuff</b>: real world mixed up with netherlings<br><b>Fail</b>: humans, school, Jeb, Jeb...Jeb.<br><b>WOW</b>: Morpheus, still and always<br><b>POV</b>: 1st-person, female<br><b>Love-Geometry</b>: medium going to hard<br><br><b>Quote-Core</b>: <blockquote>
  <i>
    “You are part human, and an artist. Creation is your power.” 
  </i>
</blockquote><br>If you’re not going to Wonderland, Wonderland is coming to you.<br><br>Yes, in this part of the trilogy we will suffer in human realm. Why suffer? You know, it’s like mixing up exquisite dish with something humble, or coffee and tea in one cup. Not tasty, not to say disgusting. People in here are boring, Alyssa’s family, Jeb (especially Jeb), her school (I’m so tired of reading about school-days, that’s why I dislike realistic ya-contemp). What looks normal among madness stuff, looks ridiculous among common things.<br><br>The only bright spot in this mess was Morpheus, okay Rabid and Chessie as well (they are sooo cute, I can’t even). I found myself skipping passages without nethelings and hating Jeb more and more, I wanted smack Alyssa too. Double standards! Finally, she got that she uses double standards: Jeb is always her knight and hero, Morpheus – cunning bastard (well, he is, but it's not that he can't be a knight at the same time). <br><br>I see why Morpheus is so fond of Alyssa. But I don’t know why Jeb is. I mean, SO fond? They are young and they have lives ahead. He’s stupid enough to believe that he’ll spent his entire life with a girl? This one particular girl? And if you think that Jeb became less possessive, you're wrong. Hands off, she’s mine, don’t look at her and suchlike things are here. Alyssa learns from him ‘cause she, too, starts to repeat MINE. I wanna kill them both.<br><br>The plot was complex once again but not enough. And all these prom balls… I’m fed up. So why 4 (out of 10) stars and not 1? Morpheus, of course. His sexy humor, the way he acts and talks, the way he looks. You can’t help your fall for him. <br><br>Look what he is doing here:<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>
      “Fair warning, I intend to make good use of that time. I will be gentle, but I will not be a gentleman. You will be the center of my world. I’ll show you the wonders of Wonderland, and when you’re drunk on the beauty and chaos that your heart so yearns to know, I will take you under my wings and make you forget the human realm ever existed. You’ll never want to leave Wonderland or me again.”
    </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  
    <i>
      <b>“Of all the times you’ve undressed me in my fantasies, I never remember feeling this … unfulfilled.” “Please, Morpheus,” I beg upon hearing Jeb stir in the background. “Ah, but those delectable words,” Morpheus says with a provocative smirk, “those are always in the fantasy.” I glare at him. “You’re unbelievable.” “And that sentiment is reserved for the end.” “Shut. Up.”</b>
    </i>
  
</blockquote><br>Such a shame the book is not about him only.<br><br>The next part of this series will bring us to AnyElsewhere, looking-glass world, so I think something interesting still has chance to happen . <br><br>I have some feelings about the ending, I hope where wouldn’t be TID’s final, though I guess this is exactly what’s going to be.<br><br><b>PS</b>: Natalia, you were right, Morpheus’s masquerade costume is a thing xDDD<br><br><b>PPS</b>: This is Leigh (not Bardugo though) from Amour Sucre, he reminds me about Morpheus a bit. Didn’t find the author of this pic, but have to thank him or her)<br><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-HKSkjhoJSOA/Vkb_EbYSFSI/AAAAAAAAAPk/Aee88bb0hoY/s1600/prince_by_leejun35-d4uym96.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447498924i/17013368.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><br><br><b>Splintered (Разделенная надвое):</b><br><blockquote>— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1100477870" rel="nofollow noopener">Splintered (Разделенная надвое)</a> #1/3<br>— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1100479578" rel="nofollow noopener">The Moth in the Mirror (Мотылек в зеркале)</a> #1.5/3<br>— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1100478586" rel="nofollow noopener">Unhinged (Слетевшая с катушек)</a> #2/3<br>— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1100478800" rel="nofollow noopener">Ensnared (Угодившая в сети)</a> #3/3<br>— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1475118683" rel="nofollow noopener">Untamed (Неукрощенная)</a> #3.5/3</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="14847730650171268357" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1162570014" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1162570014" />
    <a title="Toni" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24617462-toni"><img alt="Toni" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1162570014?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Toni" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Toni" href="/user/show/24617462-toni">Toni</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781419710476" href="/book/show/19430954-unhinged">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24617462-toni?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1162570014" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9784686867623041353"><b>3 1/2</b><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“In this realm, lighting footsteps while erasing them would be impossible and nonsensical, but not in Wonderland. And now that Wonderland has crossed our borders, it’s reasonable and makes perfect sense here.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>There is a simple way to describe this book: <b>Identity crisis.</b><br/><br/>In book one Alyssa visited Wonderland, in <i>Unhinged</i> it came back to haunt her. Making her struggle to choose between her human self or her wild, netherling side.<br/><br/>First of all- I love the story. <i>Howard</i> has a talent for writi</span>
  <span id="freeText9784686867623041353" style="display:none"><b>3 1/2</b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>“In this realm, lighting footsteps while erasing them would be impossible and nonsensical, but not in Wonderland. And now that Wonderland has crossed our borders, it’s reasonable and makes perfect sense here.”</i>
</b><br><br>There is a simple way to describe this book: <b>Identity crisis.</b><br><br>In book one Alyssa visited Wonderland, in <i>Unhinged</i> it came back to haunt her. Making her struggle to choose between her human self or her wild, netherling side.<br><br>First of all- I love the story. <i>Howard</i> has a talent for writing, it's obvious. I'm completely satisfied with her use of Lewis Carroll's original <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24213.Alice_s_Adventures_in_Wonderland___Through_the_Looking_Glass" title="Alice's Adventures in Wonderland &amp; Through the Looking-Glass by Lewis Carroll" rel="nofollow noopener">Alice's Adventures in Wonderland &amp; Through the Looking-Glass</a>. What I'm not so satisfied with? The damn love triangle.<br><br><b>I'm so sick of love triangles.</b> It's not necessary. We get that the guys <i>reflect</i> different sides of her personality. But it's supremely annoying. Especially because the less developed character is somehow the usual endgame.<br><br>And the angst overtaking the plot? Just no.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431691436ra/14860208.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Which love triangles are the hardest to handle? The ones in which you hate one character and love the other.<br><br>Jeb is not a character I would ever like. He is too perfect, written with too little flaws (and the ones that are obviously there no one acknowledges), which I find to be a huge flaw in itself.<br><br><i>"a young mortal man with a noble heart"</i><br><br>Yes, if you by noble mean: He dated the girl who bullied Alyssa, to forget her, because he loved her, and there was no good reason why he couldn't just <i>date</i> her. <br><br>No, I'm not forgetting about that one. Stupid actions in the name of "selflessness" are just that. Stupid.<br><br><b>MORPHEUS</b> on the other hand is (besides the Wonderland creatures) the only character I actually like. He is far from perfect but so well developed. He charmed me once again. Plus there's always the wit.<br><br><i>
  <b>“Fair warning, I intend to make good use of that time. I will be gentle, but I will not be a gentleman. You will be the center of my world. I’ll show you the wonders of Wonderland, and when you’re drunk on the beauty and chaos that your heart so yearns to know, I will take you under my wings and make you forget the human realm ever existed. You’ll never want to leave Wonderland or me again.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431692998ra/14860364.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The appearances of the Wonderland characters were some of my favorite things in the book. And let me just squeak at the cuteness of Chessie.<br><br>The plot is not as good as in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12558285.Splintered__Splintered___1_" title="Splintered (Splintered, #1) by A.G. Howard" rel="nofollow noopener">Splintered</a>, not boring though. The world building is lovely and miles better than in most YA books. <b>SO MUCH IMAGINATION.</b><br><br>Alyssa got on my nerves quite a bit. So much could be solved if she just <i>did</i> more. This is not the time for love drama. She is not a character I dislike (okay maybe a little bit), but she is also not a character I like either.<br><br><b>THAT ENDING THOUGH.</b> Well done.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9784686867623041353" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13728687590043097671">Curiouser and curiouser.<br/><br/>Just when you thought Alice In Wonderland couldn't possibly get any curiouser. Lewis Caroll made it mad to begin with. Animated movies made it madder. Tim Burton... I don't even know what THAT was.<br/><br/>But this, ah. This is a special kind of mad. And curious. And A.G. Howard is my favorite Mad Hatter.</span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_11300302'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11300302-alice-in-zombieland"><img alt="Alice in Zombieland (White Rabbit Chronicles, #1)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1333628241l/11300302._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('N6mRjkHyZVOim8nKPPfDndOYWYceAvh+0ms23siTG24pcPRamTsawBm1Mfg9RcifN6r+m3wQOxPTxgi8Zkdo1g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

Howard rates books on GoodReads:<br/><br/>"I only rate or review books I enjoyed reading, and w</span>
  <span id="freeText9003813997307343383" style="display:none">#1 New York Times and International bestselling Author of gothic / fantasy &amp; paranormal tales, mystical &amp; romantic with a side of horror. A.G.'s dark Alice in Wonderland inspired Splintered series has been published in over a dozen languages. <br /><br />Young adult, Adult, and literary romance. Repped by Jenny Bent.<br /><br />How A.G. Howard rates books on GoodReads:<br /><br />"I only rate or review books I enjoyed reading, and won't give any rating below 4 stars. Please don't consider every high rating a personal endorsement / recommendation from me. My ratings here are subjective to me as an individual. <br /><br />I don't rate books solely on style. Every writer's voice is individual and unique; I've come to respect this truth during my own personal journey. As long as a story takes me to another place and is well edited, I'm going to give it a good rating. And if, for some reason, a book doesn't entertain me or I don't finish it, I won't leave a rating or review at all. <br /><br />If you're considering a book I've reviewed/rated, be sure to read other reviews/ratings alongside mine to help you decide if it's a read you might enjoy personally.<br /><br />Happy book hunting!"<br /><br /></span>
